[2;36m                    [0m         known as directory traversal[1m)[0m where a malicious archive file can exploit relative   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         directory. The vulnerability was discovered during fuzz testing when attempting to  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unpack an archive containing an entry with the path                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"q/r/s/t/../../jazzer-traversal"[0m, which would resolve to a location outside the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         designated output directory.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The issue represents a **File Path Traversal vulnerability** [1m([0malso known as         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Directory Traversal or Path Traversal[1m)[0m, which is classified as a critical security  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         issue. This type of vulnerability allows an attacker to access or write files in    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directories outside of the restricted/intended directory structure.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Key Technical Details:**                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **Vulnerability Detection**: The security issue was caught by Jazzer's           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         FilePathTraversal sanitizer at runtime, which monitors file operations and detects  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attempts to access files outside permitted boundaries.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Exploitation Path**: The traversal occurs during the extraction of embedded    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         documents from an archive file. The malicious path [32m"q/r/s/t/../../jazzer-traversal"[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         uses relative path notation to navigate up the directory tree from the intended     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extraction location [32m"/tmp/expander-tmp16842528877713905477/output/"[0m.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Call Stack Analysis**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sequence:                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mTikaCLI.main[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Entry point for command-line interface                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mTikaCLI.process[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Main processing logic                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `TikaCLI$[1;35mOutputType.process[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Output type handling                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mAutoDetectParser.parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Parser detection and invocation                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mPackageParser.parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and related methods → Archive parsing logic            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `TikaCLI$[1;35mFileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.parseEmbedded[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → **Critical point     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         where file output is initiated**                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Affected Components**:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The primary vulnerability exists in the file extraction logic within           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `TikaCLI$[1;35mFileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.parseEmbedded[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method [1m([0mline [1;36m1111[0m[1m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `PackageParser` class and its methods [1m([0m`parseEntry`, `parseEntries`,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `_parse`[1m)[0m are involved in processing archive entries                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The issue affects the handling of embedded documents within package/archive    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         files                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Areas Requiring Investigation:**                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **TikaCLI$FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor Class**: Specifically the                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method at line [1;36m1111[0m, which handles the extraction of embedded     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         documents to the filesystem. This is where the vulnerable file writing operation    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         occurs.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **PackageParser Implementation**: The methods `[1;35mparseEntry[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, `[1;35mparseEntries[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and `[1;35m_parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` should be examined to understand how file paths from archive entries [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         are processed and passed to the extraction logic.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Path Validation Logic**: The codebase should be reviewed to identify where [1m([0mif [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         at all[1m)[0m path validation and sanitization is performed before file operations. The   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         absence or inadequacy of such validation is the root cause of this vulnerability.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **TikaCLI Output Handling**: The `TikaCLI$[1;35mOutputType.process[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method and       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         related output handling code should be reviewed to understand the overall file      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extraction workflow and where security controls should be enforced.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. **File Path Construction**: Any code that constructs file paths for extracted    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         content, particularly code that combines base directories with paths from archive   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries, should be scrutinized for proper path canonicalization and validation.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The vulnerability allows malicious archive files to write extracted content to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         arbitrary locations on the filesystem [1m([0mwithin the permissions of the running        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         process[1m)[0m, which could lead to unauthorized file creation, overwriting of sensitive  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         files, or potentially code execution if executable files are planted in sensitive   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         locations.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability exists in `TikaCLI.java`'s [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.getOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1128[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1169[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical issue is:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Untrusted Input Flow**: Archive entry names from `PackageParser` flow through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata without sanitization[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insufficient Normalization**: `[0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1141[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalizes paths but doesn't prevent path traversal[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Missing Validation**: No verification that the constructed `outputFile` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains within `extractDir` after path resolution[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Dangerous Directory Creation**: Parent directories are created unconditionally[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1108[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, enabling writes outside the intended directory[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Chain[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchive Entry Name [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"q/r/s/t/../../jazzer-traversal"[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mPackageParser.handleEntryMetadata[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39monly replaces backslashes[0m[1;39m][0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY metadata[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mTikaCLI.getOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnormalizes but doesn't validate[0m[1;39m][0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir, normalizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mconstructs potentially dangerous path[0m[1;39m][0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFileOutputStream creation [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwrites outside extractDir[0m[1;39m][0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference Solution[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already contains the correct pattern in `FileSystemFetcher.java` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mp = [0m[1;35mbasePath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfetchKey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mp.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mbasePath.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"fetchKey must resolve to be a descendant of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mthe 'basePath'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Patch Location: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaCLI.java`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch Point [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add path validation in `[0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1160[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert validation immediately after `File outputFile = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` and before the file existence check:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Convert both `extractDir` and `outputFile` to canonical paths[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Verify that the canonical `outputFile` path starts with the canonical [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`extractDir` path[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Throw `IOException` if validation fails with a security-focused error message[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Details:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `[0m[1;35mFile.getCanonicalPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mFile.getCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to resolve all [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymbolic links and relative path components [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`.`, `..`[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `[0m[1;35mPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for hierarchical path comparison[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This must be done BEFORE creating parent directories [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmove the validation before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m1103[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrap in try-catch to handle `IOException` from `[0m[1;35mgetCanonicalPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch Point [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Reorder operations in `[0m[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method**[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurrently the flow is:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Get outputFile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1100[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Create parent directories [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1108[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Write file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1111[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange to:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Get outputFile with validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1100[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validation now happens inside [0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Create parent directories [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1108[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Write file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1111[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specific Code Changes:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn `[0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, after line [0m[1;36m1160[0m[39m, add:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFile outputFile = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir, normalizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Security: Prevent path traversal attacks[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    File canonicalExtractDir = [0m[1;35mextractDir.getCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    File canonicalOutputFile = [0m[1;35moutputFile.getCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Verify the output file is within the extraction directory[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcanonicalOutputFile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcanonicalExtractDir.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[32m"Security: Path traversal attempt detected. Archive entry '"[0m[39m + name + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[32m"' would resolve to '"[0m[39m + canonicalOutputFile + [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[32m"' which is outside the extraction directory '"[0m[39m + canonicalExtractDir +[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mLOG.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Path validation failed for archive entry: "[0m[39m + name, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw e;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Continue with existing file existence check[0m[33m...[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative Implementation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif canonical path resolution has issues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUse `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern from `[0m[1;35mFileSystemFetcher.isDescendant[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath extractPath = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath outputPath = [0m[1;35moutputFile.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Path traversal attempt detected in: "[0m[39m + name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: All existing path normalization logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoval, prefix stripping, URL decoding, UUID generation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Adds validation as the final security gate after all [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtransformations[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Proven Pattern**: Uses the same security pattern already implemented in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FileSystemFetcher`, demonstrating consistency with the codebase's security [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpractices[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only adds validation logic without modifying the extraction[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworkflow or API[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Clear Error Messages**: Provides security-focused error messages that aid in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdebugging and security auditing[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Handles Edge Cases**: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symbolic links resolved via canonical paths[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple levels of `..` sequences[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mixed path separators [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready handled by FilenameUtils[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Absolute paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready stripped by getPrefixLength[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Validation Does Not Break Existing Functionality[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **API Compatibility**: No changes to method signatures or return types[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Legitimate Files**: Valid archive entries that extract within the output [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory will pass validation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Error Handling**: Malicious entries are rejected with clear error messages [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39malready caught by existing try-catch at line [0m[1;36m1119[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Test Compatibility**: Existing tests using well-formed archives will continue [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto pass[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Issue [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Canonical Path Resolution on Non-Existent Files**[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mgetCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` works on non-existent files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit canonicalizes the path, not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe file[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No mitigation needed[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Issue [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Performance Impact**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Canonical path resolution has minimal overhead[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Called once per extracted file, acceptable for CLI tool[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No mitigation needed[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Issue [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Platform-Specific Path Handling**[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mFile.getCanonicalPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is platform-aware [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandles Windows/Unix paths[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Already using platform-specific path handling in existing code[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No mitigation needed[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Issue [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Symbolic Link Edge Cases**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `extractDir` itself is a symlink, `[0m[1;35mgetCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` resolves it correctly[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The validation ensures the resolved output is within the resolved extraction [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No mitigation needed[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Recommendations[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be validated against:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Normal archives with legitimate nested directories[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Archives with path traversal attempts [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/[0m[39m`, `..\\`, multiple levels[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Archives with absolute paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`, `C:\`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Archives with URL-encoded traversal sequences[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Archives with null bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready handled at line [0m[1;36m1140[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Archives with symbolic link references [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif supported by archive format[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
